232"/**\n"\
233"\n"\
234" * @file Float.h\n"\
235" * @brief\n"\
236" * Here, float will be treated as bit vector with four attributes:\n"\
237" *\n"\
238"\n"\
239" * sign: \\n\t\n"\
240" * \t> Whether it has sign or not. \\n\n"\
241" *\n"\
242"\n"\
243" * exp:\t\\n\n"\
244" * \t> Exponent. It will be considered as unsigned integer, \\n\n"\
245" * \t> Which is the exponent of the [frac]\n"\
246" *\n"\
247"\n"\
248" * expbiasp: \\n\n"\
249" * \t> Exponent bias in order to be considered as zero. \\n\n"\
250" * \t> For handling possibly negative values of [exp] (such as 0.5) \\n\n"\
251" *\n"\
252"\n"\
253" * \t> Here, the value of exponent bias is limited with following rules:\n"\
254" * \t\t- It must be (2^([expbiasp]) - 1), and you are actually setting [expbiasp].\n"\
255" * \t\t- [expbiasp] must be between 1 and [exp].\n"\
256" *\n"\
257"\n"\
258" * frac: \\n\n"\
259" * \t> The actual \"value\" for floating point.\n"\
260" *\n"\
261"\n"\
262" * ==================\n"\
263" *\n"\
264"\n"\
265" * Following is the expected structure as bit vector: \\n\n"\
266" * [frac | exp | sign]\n"\
267" * \n"\
268" * Size of this will be calculated as: \\n\n"\
269" * [sign] + [exp] + [frac]\n"\
270" */\n"\
271"\n"\
272"#ifndef ae2f_Float_h\n"\
273"#define ae2f_Float_h\n"\

362"/// @brief\n"\

364"#define ae2f_errGlob_OK 0\n"\

366"/// @brief\n"\
367"/// Failed to find the function on preprocessor which is callable for some reason\n"\
368"/// No operation has beed done.\n"\
369"#define ae2f_errGlob_IMP_NOT_FOUND 0b1\n"\
370"\n"\
371"/// @brief\n"\

376"/// Failed freeing the memory.\n"\

381"#define ae2f_errGlob_ALLOC_FAILED 0b1000\n"\
382"\n"\
383"/// @brief\n"\
384"/// Found that parameter sent by programmer is invalid.\n"\
385"/// The operation may have been ceased while the middle.\n"\
386"#define ae2f_errGlob_WRONG_OPERATION 0b10000\n"\
387"\n"\
388"/// @brief\n"\
389"/// Found some errors, but not by parameters.\n"\
390"/// The operation has failed.\n"\
391"#define ae2f_errGlob_NFOUND 0b100000\n"\
392"\n"\
393"/// @brief\n"\
394"/// Means that error was not critical.\n"\
395"/// \n"\
396"/// The operation went done. \\n\n"\
397"/// Note that operation may not be valid.\n"\
398"#define ae2f_errGlob_DONE_HOWEV 0b1000000\n"\
399"\n"\
400"/// @brief\n"\
401"/// Check if the state code is a critical error.\n"\
402"/// @param n {ae2f_err_t} Error code\n"\
403"/// @return If it is not zero, it is a critical error.\n"\
404"#define ae2f_errGlobNormalised(n) (((n) & ae2f_errGlob_DONE_HOWEV) ? ae2f_errGlob_OK : (n))\n"\

3060"/**\n"\
3061"\n"\
3062" * @file Float.h\n"\
3063" * @brief\n"\
3064" * Here, float will be treated as bit vector with four attributes:\n"\
3065" *\n"\
3066"\n"\
3067" * sign: \\n\t\n"\
3068" * \t> Whether it has sign or not. \\n\n"\
3069" *\n"\
3070"\n"\
3071" * exp:\t\\n\n"\
3072" * \t> Exponent. It will be considered as unsigned integer, \\n\n"\
3073" * \t> Which is the exponent of the [frac]\n"\
3074" *\n"\
3075"\n"\
3076" * expbiasp: \\n\n"\
3077" * \t> Exponent bias in order to be considered as zero. \\n\n"\
3078" * \t> For handling possibly negative values of [exp] (such as 0.5) \\n\n"\
3079" *\n"\
3080"\n"\
3081" * \t> Here, the value of exponent bias is limited with following rules:\n"\
3082" * \t\t- It must be (2^([expbiasp]) - 1), and you are actually setting [expbiasp].\n"\

4353" * \t\t- It must be (2^([expbiasp]) - 1), and you are actually setting [expbiasp].\n"\

5876" * @file Float.h\n"\

5881" * sign: \\n\t\n"\

5894"\n"\
